Important Foreign News

Unprecedented Disaster in Lyon: Following Floods, Landslides Occur 61

Twenty-Two Houses Collapse; Over One Hundred Casualties

Paris, 13th (Agence Nationale) - A flood occurred in the city of Lyon today, collapsing twenty-two houses. The known death toll is eighty, but the total number of casualties is estimated to be over one hundred. In recent days, Lyon has experienced continuous heavy rain, and residents have been fearful of the Rhone and Saône rivers overflowing. As expected, at 1:00 AM this morning, the river water collapsed a surrounding wall and came crashing down like a landslide. Houses and livestock were unable to escape in time and were swept away and drowned. Cries for help arose everywhere, and warnings were issued continuously. The police force rushed to the scene and tried their best to block the flood. While rescue work was underway, landslides suddenly occurred, and twenty-two houses collapsed instantly. Twelve firefighters, seventeen police officers, and two doctors at the scene were tragically crushed to death. Troops stationed throughout the city have now been dispatched to the disaster area to try their best to prevent the disaster from spreading, and to assist nearby residents in relocating to temporary shelters. Churches and schools are sheltering the displaced people, who are overflowing with crying women and wailing children, which is unbearable to witness. Some say that the tragic scenes of the European war have reappeared today.

Lyon, 13th (Reuters) - At 1:00 AM this morning, a wall collapsed on a street in this area. The fire department and police rushed to the rescue, but two more houses collapsed in succession, burying the rescuers under the rubble. It is reported that at least sixty people were killed and forty injured. The exact numbers cannot be determined immediately. A subsequent dispatch stated that at least ten six- or seven-story residential buildings collapsed on a street in the Saint-Jean district of this town. At present, firefighters, police, and volunteers are risking their lives to rescue those buried. A subsequent dispatch stated that houses continued to collapse, and thirty bodies have been recovered so far. Except for five people, all of them were rescuers, including the fire chief and deputy chief, eighteen firefighters, and five police officers.

British Prime Minister Delivers Opening Address at Indian Round Table Conference 62

London, 12th (Reuters) - The British Prime Minister, as chairman of the Indian Round Table Conference, delivered an address stating that the people in attendance shoulder the responsibility of rewriting new history that is currently coming into existence. The British monarch and governing officials have repeatedly declared that Britain's work in India is solely to prepare India for self-government. Now we gather here to register in an agreement that India has reached the crucial points in its constitutional process, a fact that is acknowledged. However, differing opinions still need to be resolved, and conflicting interests have yet to be reconciled. This conference should resolve to address and overcome these difficulties, which is not impossible. Have we not encountered various difficulties in the growth and development of constitutional freedom? However, no matter the obstacles, we will ultimately unite. This is because we have the ability to reconcile differences through reasonable mutual forgiveness. We are now before the British monarch and should be aware of the strong and resilient chain that links the entire British Empire to a common oath of loyalty to the sovereign. The participation of representatives from the overseas dominions in this conference is proof that the sister nations of the British Empire will observe our work with goodwill and attention. The unprecedented gathering of the Indian princes and representatives of the people of British India is also a sign that India is gradually merging into a single entity. The representatives of British India, who come from different ethnic groups, religions, and interests, are well aware of this. However, they also remember the unifying forces that naturally arose after India's contact with Britain and the desire for a unified India held in the hearts of Indian philosophers and emperors before the first British merchant arrived in their territory. We sit around this table with the sole fixed purpose of enhancing India's position in the British Empire. This is a simple fact, and this alone is an undeniable sign of progress towards this goal. It is hoped that those in attendance will ensure that this conference is worthy of the British Empire's people's superior political talent.

Jamu and the King of Kashmir stated that the Indian princes, as allied states of the United Kingdom, deeply desire to be connected with Britain, and as Indians, deeply desire to enjoy honor and equality in the British Empire. The representative of Hyderabad, Haitari, stated that no one wants to sever the chain connecting the British monarch and the princes. At the same time, the princes are prepared to work with the people of British India in harmony to achieve the realization of a unified and great India. The Muslim representative, Jinnah, stated that India now hopes that the declaration of the Viceroy of India on October 31st, which stated that the natural result of India's constitutional progress would be the acquisition of dominion status, will become a reality and be implemented. We are very pleased that representatives from the overseas dominions have come to participate in this conference, as they are here today to witness the birth of a new dominion in the British Empire (the audience applauded loudly). The Burmese representative, Ba Bo, stated that he hopes that Burma will soon be an equal partner with other dominions in the British Empire.

Taiwanese Aborigines Continue Counterattacks 63

Wushe, 12th (Dentsu) - Sixty members of the Tataya aboriginal team were ambushed by enemy aborigines between Haban and Wushe while inspecting the enemy aborigines. Only twelve survived, and the rest were killed in action. After receiving this report, a police team and two hundred loyal aborigines immediately mobilized, but the enemy aborigines fled into the deep forest and their whereabouts could not be found. Airplanes dropped bombs to attack the main force of the enemy aborigines hiding in the caves of the Mahebo community, which seemed to have a considerable effect.

Revolutionary Turmoil in Cuba: Students and Police Clash Frequently 64

Havana, 12th (Associated Press) - Six hundred students clashed with police officers in the Havana newspaper building today, and one student was injured. Today's turmoil was just one of a series of incidents in recent days. At present, this kind of turmoil in Cuba is becoming increasingly serious and almost pervasive throughout the island, and it is particularly intense in the cities.

Disarmament Conference Continues Debate on Limiting Land Warfare Equipment 65

Representatives from Britain, France, and the United States Propose Draft

Geneva, 12th (Agence Nationale) - After a long period of intense debate, the Disarmament Preparatory Committee's discussion on the issue of limiting land warfare equipment has been adjourned until Thursday for further deliberation. The Japanese representative Sato, the French representative Mai Sheni, and representatives from Romania, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and other countries all opposed direct limitations. Italy, Germany, the Netherlands, Sweden, Norway, and Soviet Russia supported direct limitations. The Soviet representative Litvinov also requested indirect limitations in the budget in addition to direct limitations.

Geneva, 13th (Reuters) - The Disarmament Committee resumed its discussion today on methods for setting land armament restrictions. Lord Cecil, on behalf of the British, French, and American delegations, put forward a draft in three parts. First, it supports the principle that all countries acceding to the current convention should exchange information on armaments as much as possible. Second, it records the committee's desire to seek a consistent method of limiting war materiel in a more definitive state than mere publication. Third, it recognizes the majority opinion of the committee that the most appropriate method of limiting land armaments is budgetary restrictions. Others believe that a more effective method is direct restrictions and categorization, and some advocate using both methods. After discussion, the committee verbally amended and adopted the first and second items, and decided to discuss the third item again on the 14th to allow British and German representatives to negotiate verbal amendments.

Page 7

Important Foreign News Two

Overview of the French National Defense 66

National Service Army Term Reduced to One Year; Total National Army Strength Planned at 520,000

Paris dispatch: The law, approved by the French Parliament the year before last (1928), to reduce the compulsory military service period for conscripts to twelve months has been implemented since November 1st of this year. This is the first such instance since the French Revolution. According to this law, the national army will be reduced by over ten thousand men. Since Germany was bound by the Treaty of Versailles to reduce its army, it has adopted a strategy of elite troops, based on the principle that a small number of well-trained soldiers can be rapidly mobilized and launched an attack. Former German Army Commander Seeckt once said that he believed this was the most suitable military strategy for future wars. French military authorities, recognizing Germany's success, decided to follow suit and began to reorganize the original army organization law on a trial basis. However, this aroused opposition from nationalist factions, who said that Germany's threat was becoming increasingly clear, while France was still talking about reducing its army, which was absurd. They did not understand that the authorities were reducing the size of the army without impairing its quality. The military budget in the 1931 budget increased by 75 million francs compared to the previous year, so although the number of personnel has decreased, the army's strength has only increased. The determination of French Minister of War Maginot to reform the system stemmed from the large-scale exercises held in the border regions of Germany and Italy in the summer and autumn of this year. The total number of people who participated in these exercises reached about 100,000, and it was deeply felt that the large number of people made command difficult and maneuverability inflexible, lacking the value of surprise in attack. Therefore, it was decided to reform the system. The budget for the number of soldiers serving one-year terms nationwide was reduced to 523,769, which is not much different from the 556,000 announced by Briand at the League of Nations in Geneva. Compared with the 810,000 at the outbreak of the Great War, this is a reduction of 41 percent. The organizational content is: conscripts (French) 240,000, North African native troops 95,000, other colonial native troops 84,000, and professional soldiers 16,000. According to Maginot's plan, 200,000 men are to be used as vanguard troops, and the remaining 300,000 men as rear defense troops. In addition, France has built numerous solid defense projects at the borders with Germany, Italy, Belgium, and other countries. Construction began two years ago and is expected to be completed within seven years, with a total cost of approximately 7 billion francs (approximately 70 million US dollars). National defense can be said to be extremely thorough, but opponents of a small army still maintain that German troops are actually stronger than French troops in terms of combat power. Although the peace treaty stipulates that only 100,000 troops are allowed to defend the eastern border, Germany's armed police force nationwide reaches 150,000, and they are well-trained and can be deployed for external operations at any time. France, on the other hand, only has 106,000 professional soldiers, and only 46,000 are stationed in France. As for conscripts, only 90,000 are combat-ready in a given period. Therefore, compared to Germany, it is only a ratio of 136,000 to 250,000. However, this reason is not sufficient, as most of the French soldiers stationed abroad are in North Africa, and it only takes two days to return to their homeland in case of emergency. Furthermore, French military authorities are paying close attention to the latest killing techniques using scientific methods. According to experts, France is still far behind Germany in this regard. (World)

Preparatory Meeting of the Opium Conference Concludes 67

Agreement Reached on Allocation Methods for Raw Opium Quotas

Reuters, London, December 12: The preparatory meeting of the Opium Conference concluded today, having agreed on temporary methods for allocating raw opium manufacturing quotas among manufacturing countries. As for the allocation of quotas for morphine and other substances, representatives of the governments concerned will continue to consider the matter with a view to reaching an agreement before the meeting of the League of Nations Opium Advisory Committee in January. The plan drawn up by the preparatory meeting does not involve Turkey and Japan, as both countries reserved their decisions. Eleven countries participated in the meeting, including Great Britain, the United States, India, and Russia.

Austrian Social Democratic Party Marches and Demonstrates to Celebrate Election Victory 68

National News, Vienna, December 12: More than 60,000 members of the Socialist Party held a large demonstration today on Lin Street, the most famous street in Vienna, to celebrate the victory of the Socialist Party in Sunday's general election. The Social Democratic Party, which had always held the second-largest number of seats in Parliament, has now risen to first place. Unfortunately, Major Pabst, the leader of the quasi-fascist Heimwehr organization, who had previously been expelled from Austria by the Austrian government, has now had this order rescinded by Internal Affairs Minister Steinhauser, the leader of the Heimwehr, and has returned from Italy, where he was warmly welcomed by the leaders of the group. The masses now fear that this matter will lead to serious developments, as Steinhauser had declared before the election that regardless of the outcome of the election, the Heimwehr would not give up the power it currently holds in the government.

Student Riot at the University of Berlin 69

Rival Factions Confront Each Other with Pistols

National News, Berlin, December 12: A riot broke out at the University of Berlin today, which was not quelled until the police intervened. Initially, Social Democratic students disagreed with leaflets distributed by the National Socialist Party. National Socialist students were greatly angered and, ignoring the advice of the principal, attacked students who appeared to be Jewish. Immediately, students from both the Social Democratic and National Socialist factions gathered in the open space on campus for a major battle, even firing several shots. As a result, many male students and one female student were injured. When the police arrived at the school and wielded batons, they were able to disperse the crowd, but shortly afterward, another conflict arose due to the refusal to release seven key members of the National Socialist Party who had been arrested.

Norway Relinquishes Sovereignty over Sverdrup Island 70

National News, Oslo, December 12: It is officially confirmed that Norway has signed a treaty with Canada relinquishing sovereignty over the Sverdrup Islands. These islands, located west of Greenland, were discovered by Norwegian Sverdrup during the Second Fram Expedition. The treaty must be approved by Parliament, but the Norwegian Parliament is not expected to object, as Canada will still allow Norwegian whaling ships and fishing boats to use the islands as fishing grounds and will award Sverdrup, who is currently seriously ill, 30,000 yuan as compensation for his discovery.

German Public Opinion Greatly Angered

National News, Berlin, December 12: A New York dispatch states that the new Brazilian government does not acknowledge any responsibility for the shelling of the German merchant ship Baden, which resulted in the death of 29 people and the injury of 40 people, and refuses to compensate the families of the deceased and the shipping company. German newspapers are very indignant at this news. Nationalist newspapers claim that if this news is confirmed, Germany should immediately sever diplomatic relations with Brazil and not resume them until Brazil acknowledges compensation.

Situation of Zhang Xueliang Passing Through Jinan 74

Jinan Correspondence: Deputy Commander of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Zhang Xueliang passed through Jinan early this morning (the 11th) amidst a grand welcome from all sectors. On the evening of the 10th, Jinan received a telegram from Tianjin stating that Zhang's special train departed from Tianjin in the afternoon, with a total of three trains. The first train was a guard train, which departed from Tianjin at 5:25 PM and was expected to arrive in Jinan at 4:30 AM on the 11th. The second train was Zhang's special train, which departed from Tianjin at 6:55 PM and was scheduled to arrive in Jinan at 6:30 AM on the 11th. The third train was a staff train, which departed from Tianjin at 7:30 PM on the 10th and was scheduled to arrive in Jinan at 6:30 AM on the 11th. All sectors immediately began preparing for the welcome. The train station and various government agencies were decorated with pine branches, and the entire city was hung with national flags and various welcome slogans. The pistol brigade, public security bureau, and security team were deployed around the station and nearby areas to provide security. All representatives from various sectors were not allowed to enter the station unless they held a temporary pass issued by the provincial government. From 3:00 AM this morning (the 11th), welcoming personnel began to arrive at the station in droves. By 5:00 AM, the provincial government chairman Han Fuqu, Central Committee member Ding Weifen, National Arts Museum Director Li Jinglin, Education Department Director He Siyuan, Construction Department Director Zhang Honglie, Finance Department Director Wang Xiangrong, Jinan Mayor Chen Weixin, Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee member Zhang Weicun, Jiaoji Railway Committee Chairman Sa Fujun, Salt Transport Envoy Wang Zhanghu, Chamber of Commerce Chairman Xin Zhujiu, 94th Army Commander Cao Fulin, Pistol Brigade Commander Lei Taiping, 22nd Division Commander Gu Liangmin, Cavalry Division Commander Wang Guide, 1st Army Corps Chief of Staff Li Zongbi, and representatives from various sectors, news reporters, and others, totaling about one hundred people, had arrived. After 5:00 AM, a telegram was received from Dezhou stating that the guard train departed from Dezhou at 2:50 AM, Zhang's special train departed from Dezhou at 3:40 AM, and the staff train departed from Dezhou at 4:10 AM. When Zhang's special train passed through Dezhou, it stopped for an hour to refuel and water, but did not meet with the welcoming personnel. Subsequently, a telephone call was received from Yucheng stating that Zhang's special train passed through Yucheng at 5:30 AM and was expected to arrive in Jinan around 7:00 AM. At 6:15 AM, the first guard train arrived in Jinan, consisting of locomotive No. 166, two Jinpu third-class carriages, one Beining second-class carriage, six third-class carriages, two iron boxcars, one flatcar, one factory car, one Jing Sui third-class carriage, and one guard car, totaling fifteen cars carrying a squad of guards, four cars, and one car. The commander was Liu Duoquan, commander of the guard of the Northeast Border Defense Commander's Office. At 6:55 AM, Zhang's special train arrived in Jinan, and the military band played loudly. The soldiers on the platform saluted. The atmosphere inside the station was solemn. Zhang's special train locomotive was Beining Road No. 163, consisting of three third-class carriages, two second-class carriages, one first- and second-class mixed carriage, one special private car No. 51, four private cars, one dining car, three first-class carriages, one lounge car, one official car, one flatbed car, and one guard car, totaling twenty cars. Zhang was riding in private car No. 51. The special trains of He Yaozu, Zhang Qun, and others also came from Tianjin, attached to Zhang's train. Li Shuchun, Wang Fangting, and other representatives sent by Han Fuqu to Tianjin to welcome him also returned to Jinan on the same train. Accompanying Zhang were Central Committee members Wu Tiecheng and Zhang Ji, Central Representatives Liu Guang and Wang Shuhan, He Fenglin, Director of the General Affairs Department Zhu Guangmu, Chief Secretary Ye Biliang, Chief of Staff Bao Wenjie, Adjutant Chief Huang Xiansheng, and Chief of the Military Supply Department Su Quanbin. Mr. Zhang was wearing a yellow wool military uniform, had a short beard, and looked energetic, but his face was slightly yellow and slightly dusty. After the train stopped, the welcoming personnel presented their cards and paid their respects. Zhang immediately invited Han Fuqu, Ding Weifen, and Li Jinglin to board the train for a discussion, and the adjutant extended the invitation to all the welcoming representatives to the first-class private car No. 101. Zhang talked with Han, Ding, and others for about fifty minutes before entering the first-class private car, where he was introduced to the welcoming personnel by Han Fuqu. Zhang stood up and spoke briefly, saying that the weather was too cold and he was ashamed that everyone had come here. He said that the armed comrades of the Third Route Army, under the guidance of Xiang Fang, had fought hard for more than half a year and finally ended the military campaign, pacified the local area, and suppressed the bandits. He said that this kind of perseverance was admirable. He said that he had only had correspondence with everyone in the past, but he was very happy to meet them today. He was sorry that he could not get off the train to have a pleasant conversation with everyone because the journey was urgent and he had to rush to Nanjing to attend the birthday celebration of the Prime Minister. He said that if he had some free time after returning from Beijing, he would be happy to get off the train and stay in Jinan.

Qingdao Negotiations to Recover Japanese Fisheries Association 76

The Party and Government Are Studying Methods

Qingdao Correspondence: The Qingdao Japanese Fisheries Association was established during the Japanese occupation era. At that time, the association's rules were formulated by the Japanese military headquarters, which provided subsidies totaling more than 20,000 yuan. Japanese individuals, including Nakazato Masuki, etc., gathered funds to undertake the business, with a total capital of about 40,000 yuan. They also established a fish market and financial association at the Xiaogang Wharf. According to recent investigations, the association owns more than 50 fishing boats, including steamers and sailboats, large and small. The annual sales of fish are about 300,000 yuan. All Chinese and foreign fishermen who land fish must pay a commission of 10%. The association also designated 20 Chinese people to serve as brokers. All sales, purchases, and loans of gold pounds by Chinese fishermen are controlled by these brokers, and non-members of the association are not allowed to engage in fishing. This seriously infringes upon China's sovereignty. Therefore, after the recovery of Qingdao, Chinese merchants and civilians established the Fisheries Association and the Fisheries Federation to try to resist it, but the business failed due to poor management. The government also successively formulated regulations on banning fisheries, paying license fees, and collecting fishing taxes, but due to successive changes in leadership, they were unable to implement them thoroughly. After the establishment of the municipal government, it repeatedly sent personnel to conduct informal negotiations with the Japanese side, but the Japanese side used its vested rights as an excuse and said that according to the provisions of Article 2 of the Annex to the Shandong Case Agreement, the issue of vested rights should be clarified by China and Japan through appropriate means. According to Article 3 of the Fisheries Regulations published by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining, those who obtain fishing rights in territorial waters and public waters should apply to the government for registration in accordance with the law, but the applicant should be a Chinese citizen. The international practice is that only nationals can engage in fishing and coastal trade in territorial waters, which is consistent with the purpose of the article. Today, the Japanese Fisheries Association arbitrarily catches fish in the Qingdao coastal area, which not only infringes upon China's sovereignty but also violates international practice. It should be negotiated to cancel it in order to safeguard maritime rights. It is heard that the Municipal Guidance Committee has sent a letter to the municipal government requesting it to negotiate with the Japanese consul to recover the association. After the municipal government approved the letter, it is studying appropriate methods and will submit negotiations in the coming days. (November 11)

On October 1st of this year, the large bandit forces of Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang captured the county seat and occupied it for many days. The looting, arson, and killing were more severe than in neighboring counties. On the first day of this month, a large number of bandits from Xiajiang and Xingan folded to Yaoxu in the county (plotting to attack Shanggao Gaoan), and the situation was very fierce. The burning and killing were extremely tragic. According to refugees who detoured to Shanggao and Gaoan to the province, when the bandits concentrated in Xinyu, they divided into three detachments to attack: one detoured from Xiadong Yaoxu in the county to Huangtuzhan and Gaoan's Huibu in Qingjiang, and the Mengshan area in the county; one crossed the river from Shuikou in Henan in the county and detoured to Jieqiao Sanglin in Fenyi; and one attacked the county seat directly from Luofang in the county, and distributed them to Shuibei Jiangdong Guanchao Ouli and other places. Now, bandits are everywhere, looting and killing, and no one is spared. Moreover, they even allowed peasant bandits to seek revenge and retaliation in the villages every day, and colluded with local hooligans to set up township and district Soviet governments and peasant associations everywhere. They implemented a three-for-one and five-for-two system for able-bodied men to serve as Red Guards and vanguards. What is even more tragic is that the villagers of Hebei 48 in the county have always been known to be strong and fierce. They hated the bandits' rampage and repeatedly gathered to defend themselves, killing many bandits. The bandits hated them to the bone and retaliated extremely viciously. They would catch people and rob things when they saw them, and burn houses that were slightly new. From the first day of last month to November 5th, it is estimated that more than 2,000 houses were burned down, more than 5,000 men, women, old and young were looted, and more than 1,000 people were killed on the spot. The total local loss is about 4 million yuan, and the vitality is exhausted. It is truly an unprecedented catastrophe. To this day, the large bandits have not completely retreated, and the small bandits are even more rampant. Xinyu has been devastated, and it is not known to what extent it will stop. (November 10)

Yizhang Legal Groups Request Guangdong to Send Troops to Suppress

Guangdong Province Cracks Down on Private Coin Forgery Operation 80

More Than a Dozen Suspects Arrested in Panyu's Pingshan Village

Guangzhou Dispatch: Unlawful elements in Guangdong Province often establish private mints to produce counterfeit currency for illicit profit. Although private currency forging is strictly prohibited by national law, unscrupulous individuals, enticed by the potential for immense gain, disregard the risks. Following the dismantling of a paper currency counterfeiting operation led by Cui某 last year, authorities subsequently uncovered several private mints producing copper coins in areas like Shang Panyu and Henan. Recently, another massive private mint was discovered and dismantled in Pingshan Village, Panyu County. Earlier this month, a scholar, Mr. 某, secretly reported to the Finance Department that a local tyrant in Pingshan Village, Panyu, was secretly forging counterfeit currency on a large scale, guarded by armed personnel, making it difficult to apprehend without deploying armed forces for encirclement. Upon receiving the report, the Finance Department immediately dispatched Special Agent Chief Gao Dingrong leading a team of sixty special agents, along with Commissioners Xiao Songyou, Xiao Hanbin, and Chen Gongjie, accompanied by Inspector He Mingong from the Public Security Bureau, carrying a warrant from the Finance Department Director. The warrant stated: "Based on intelligence, Jian Bang, a local tyrant in Pingshan Village, Panyu County, is operating a factory there, illicitly forging counterfeit currency, which is highly illegal. You are hereby ordered to dispatch a team to investigate thoroughly, apprehend the suspects, and notify the local police to avoid misunderstandings. This is of utmost importance." Upon receiving the order, the officers convened at the Traffic Hotel, Room 50, on Changdi at 2 PM on the 7th to devise a plan for the raid. Given the strong security surrounding the private mint and the confusing network of small roads, the sixty special agents were barely enough to cover the area, requiring careful pre-planning and the recruitment of machine workers to dismantle the equipment. After finalizing the arrangements, they boarded small motorboats late on the night of the 7th and set off for their destination. By 4 AM on the 8th, with only a faint moonlight illuminating the sky, the soldiers landed and were immediately met with resistance. The guards on the watchtower, spotting a large group of strong men in the dead of night, sensed something amiss and opened fire to resist arrest. The special agent soldiers then divided into teams and surrounded the bandit's compound in Pingshan Village from all sides. Jian Bang, a local ruffian in the village, brazenly directed his men to resist the government forces. Initially unaware of the bandits' numbers, the government forces were unable to approach due to the bandits' heavy gunfire and were forced to return fire in an attempt to gain the upper hand. After holding their ground until dawn, it was discovered that the bandits numbered only about forty. The government forces then launched a full-scale assault, infiltrating the compound through side routes. The bandits, losing their fortifications, abandoned their weapons and fled. Government forces captured more than ten people on the spot, wounding two. The main culprit, Jian Bang, disguised himself among the bandits and escaped, evading capture. However, his wife, Jian Han氏, was apprehended in Jian's mansion. Six mint locations were discovered nearby, yielding approximately twenty loads of private minted silver coin machinery and thousands of counterfeit coin blanks, along with large baskets of copper sheets. More than forty laborers were hired to transport the goods back to the provincial capital. Additionally, more than ten bandits were escorted to the Finance Department. The suspects included Jian Han氏, 30 years old, from Panyu; Zeng Funian, 45 years old; Yuan Chi, 35 years old; Ye Rong Sheng, 21 years old; Liang Yao, 27 years old; Liang Run, 41 years old; Chen Ying, 32 years old; Lin Jin Gu, 20 years old; Lin Xitian, 28 years old, all from Panyu; Liang Sen, 20 years old, from Shunde; and Chen Tian, from Kaiping. Fan Yi, 31 years old, from Panyu, sustained a gunshot wound; Zhou Xian suffered a facial gunshot wound and fell heavily from the roof, sustaining severe injuries that may be life-threatening. Additionally, two gentry members suspected of harboring the criminals, Huang Bachen and Jian Jianmin, were also apprehended. The group was escorted to the Finance Department at 4 PM on the 8th for interrogation by the trial division. (Evening of November 8th)

National Government and Northeast China Dispatch Special Commissioners to Sino-Russian Conference 81

Shenyang Dispatch: Following the opening of the Sino-Russian conference, the proceedings stalled due to Russia's insistence on the Khabarovsk Protocol. Initial reports indicated that the National Government would dispatch four special commissioners to Russia to assist Mo Dehui, but there has been no further news. Upon investigation, it was learned that the so-called four special commissioners were in fact two commissioners each dispatched by the National Government and the Northeast. The National Government has appointed Qian Tai from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Mr. Zhu, while the Northeast has appointed Wang Mingchen, the current secretary of the Frontier Affairs Office, and Zhang Shou Zeng, the director of the Heihe Municipal Preparatory Office. Zhang was summoned by telegraph and departed from Heihe on the 20th of last month, arriving in Harbin on the 29th after nine days of travel. He arrived in Shenyang on the 1st of this month and is staying at the Kaining Hotel on Sanjing Road. On the 8th, a reporter interviewed Mr. Zhang, who stated that he was one of the four special commissioners dispatched to Russia. His departure date is contingent upon the arrival of Qian and Zhu from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Shenyang, with whom Wang Mingchen, dispatched from this region, will travel. The date for departure to Russia is therefore uncertain. Although news of the conference has been scarce, it is unlikely to collapse. Mo's earlier proposal to return to China has been completely abandoned, and the prospects for the conference remain optimistic. We are being dispatched to Russia to assist Representative Mo in various negotiations. Furthermore, Mo's view is that as the plenipotentiary representative appointed by the National Government, he must follow the orders of the National Government. The National Government and the Northeast have consistently adopted a unified approach to the conference issue. As for the policies to be adopted by our side after the resumption of the conference, they can be determined after Deputy Commander Zhang meets with Chairman Jiang. Our actions can also be determined by this. Shipping between Heihe and Russia has resumed, with the shipping agreement signed by local authorities and the Russian side. The market is also peaceful. (November 9th)

Plague Eradicated Along the Siping-Taonan Railway 82

Shenyang Dispatch: The customs along the Siping-Taonan Railway are crude and sanitation is generally neglected. Every year around July and August, outbreaks of plague are recorded. Although the Northeast Epidemic Prevention Office cooperates with local officials to prevent the spread and the Siping-Taonan Railway Bureau provides assistance, the plague is rampant, resulting in countless deaths and requiring significant time to eradicate. In August of this year, an epidemic broke out in Tongjiawopu, Gaiduan, Halagan, and Eight Faces Mountain Zhaodong villages and townships in Kaitong County, resulting in the deaths of thirteen men and women within days. Symptoms included headaches, coldness of the heart, mental confusion, and swollen buboes on the thighs. Doctors of both Western and Chinese medicine diagnosed the illness as the same as the epidemic of the previous autumn and confirmed the presence of bubonic plague after examining the blood of the infected. Epidemics also broke out in Hao Tu Tai and other villages in the third and fifth districts of the county, resulting in dozens of deaths. Furthermore, eight deaths from bubonic plague were recorded in Shuiquan Village in the Tuenquan region northwest of Taonan County. The Liaoning Provincial Government repeatedly ordered the Shenyang Municipal Hospital and the Northeast Epidemic Prevention Office to dispatch capable personnel for prevention and treatment and to properly plan prevention measures. Corpses and rooms were disinfected and burned, and car tickets for Kaitong Station and other places were suspended for several days. Carbolic acid and other items were purchased for door-to-door disinfection and strict quarantine. Cases of the plague were immediately reported to the city by the district sub-offices, and doctors were dispatched for diagnosis and treatment. Temporary epidemic prevention and inspection stations and epidemic isolation centers were also established in Qian Fanzhi's district, and the treatment of the epidemic was gradually undertaken by medical officers, and the epidemic gradually subsided. Statistics showed approximately one hundred deaths before and after. Currently, no deaths have been reported for the past half-month, transportation has been restored, and the epidemic has been completely eradicated. (November 9th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 83

Summary of Arson and Murder Cases by Bandits in Southern Songjiang: Last night (the 12th), the areas of Xiahengjing, Donggaobao, and Xiangjia in southern Songjiang County were suddenly attacked by more than a dozen bandits speaking local and Hakka dialects, who looted freely, causing significant losses before fleeing with their stolen goods. Additionally, the families of Yang Banming and Zhang Mihou in Mapengtou, near the same area, were robbed on the night of the 3rd. Furthermore, the house of Shen Xiaomao in Jinshan County, Jialian Li'an, was also visited by twenty bandits on the same night, who robbed them of the proceeds from the sale of cotton and jewelry. Before leaving, they instructed the victims to prepare funds and return in three days, making threatening remarks. Three days later, the bandits returned to demand the previous ransom. However, after being robbed, the victims suffered severe losses and were unable to raise the large sum demanded. Enraged, the bandits set fire to their residence, which spread to neighboring homes, before leaving. On the night of the 9th, Hu Haoyun's house in the same village was also robbed, and his wife was shot and killed. The case has already been reported to the county government for investigation and arrest. The rampant banditry in southern Songjiang is evident.

Wuxi 84

Special Tax Bureau Auctions Smuggled Cloth Boat: The inspection boat of the Wuxi Cotton Weaving Special Tax Bureau recently intercepted a boat carrying white cloth from a certain cloth factory in Huashu Town, Jiangyin County, near Gaoqiao. The value of the cloth was significant. The boat was immediately seized and taken to the Huangbudun Inspection Office, where it was reported to the Special Tax Bureau and forwarded to the General Bureau for confiscation. Approval has already been granted. If anyone wishes to purchase the cloth, it will be sold at 80% of the market price. If the original factory purchases the entire amount, it will be sold at a further 80% discount as a special consideration.

Kidnapping Case: Ransom Demanded for Land Deed: Hua Jinhan's family, a wealthy household in Lian Rong Town, North Seventh Room Dongjie, District 15 (Qing City), was robbed on the night of the 6th around 10 PM. Land deeds and other items were stolen. Before leaving, the bandits also kidnapped Hua's concubine, Wu, and his eldest daughter, Xiangying. The two hostages were released the next day and returned home. It is said that the bandits took Hua's concubine and daughter to Panluotang Bridge that night (about three or four li from Qingyang Town, Cheng County), which is an extremely remote area with several dilapidated houses. The bandits ordered the two to stay in the house. Hua's concubine and daughter were extremely anxious and cried uncontrollably. An old woman from a small village next to the dilapidated house heard the crying and went to inquire. The two women told her the whole story. The old woman said, "I have decided to send you two back first, don't be sad. But after you return home, quickly prepare 7,000 yuan to redeem the land deeds (totaling 320 mu). Don't delay, or else there will be consequences." After saying this, she ordered two bandits to take the Hua women to Huangdu Place by boat and put them ashore. The two then hired a fishing boat and returned home. Afterwards, it was speculated that the old woman might be the mother of the bandit leader. Currently, Hua Jinhan is still hesitant about redeeming the land deeds.

Changshu 85

Shanghai Tobacco Factory Salesman Robbed in Changshu: The Shanghai Tangshan Road Xincheng Cigarette Factory recently sent a salesman, Zhao Shouxin, with various types of cigarettes on a boat to Kunshan and Changshu to promote sales. On the night of the 9th, the boat sailed to Niujing, at the border of Kunshan and Changshu. Because it was late, they stopped for the night. Unexpectedly, at midnight, a boat of bandits approached and cut the mooring rope, drifting the boat three or four li to a remote place outside of Niujing. Seven or eight strong bandits boarded the boat and robbed them, taking all the goods, more than 400 yuan, and more than 100 yuan from the crew. Zhao immediately sailed the boat to Changshu overnight, docking at Fanjiashi in Xiaodongmen, and reported the incident to the water and land police, requesting them to pursue the bandits. He also reported the incident to the Shanghai headquarters by long-distance telephone.

Jiashan 86

Guards Arrest Kidnappers: The city defense force received a report on the afternoon of the 10th that kidnappers were hiding in Chenjiawan in the countryside near Lizhai Town. They immediately led a team to arrest six bandits and seized two pistols and a boy hostage, who was from Liantang Town, Jiangsu Province. They were all taken to the city for interrogation. It was learned that the owner of a teahouse located on the east side of Xiaosiquiao outside the East Gate was also involved in the kidnapping, so the teahouse owner was also arrested. They were transferred to the county government on the 11th for strict handling.

Township Police Gambling and Arrested in Tianren District: Wu Baosheng, a township police officer in Tianni Village Town, used the name of celebration to gamble on the 6th of this month. The incident was secretly reported to the county government by the town's gentry and civilians. County Magistrate Liang specially instructed Police Chief Yan to send a patrol officer to lead the police to investigate. The chief of the town's public security bureau was also at the township police officer's house for a banquet. Two mahjong tiles were found, taken to the bureau, and reported to County Magistrate Liang. Township police officer Wu Baosheng was found to be gambling and taking cuts, which is illegal, and the town's bureau chief was found to have not detained him and instead to be involved, which taints his official conduct. It is proposed to report to the provincial office for review and disciplinary action.

Jiaxing 87

High Court Orders Investigation into Death of Prisoner: Jiaxing Third Prison this summer early had prison riots arise from cutting off prisoner provisions and maltreating prisoners. After the former County Magistrate came to the prison to persuade, everything was alright, and also commanded the warden to improve prisoner treatment. Because between September and October this year over five prisoners have died the High Court fears prisoner’s death are related, and specially ordered Jiaxing Local Branch Court to investigate. So the Branch Court arrested four prisoners Jiang Fenglin, Zhang Debao, Wang Dasheng, and Wu Xiugen late last night to investigate everything. Theft and Robbery in Daqiao Township: More than ten thieves broke into the house of farmer Shen Erguan in Daqiao Township, about three miles outside the North Gate of Jiaxing, the night before last. Shen Erguan was dragged outside the house and brutally beaten, while another group broke into the inner room and searched arbitrarily. After neighboring villagers sounded an alarm, the thieves collected their loot and left. After taking stock of the stolen items, it was estimated that the stolen clothing, ornaments, and other items were worth about 300 yuan. The incident has been reported to the authorities for investigation and arrest.

Huzhou 88

Dispute over Display of Artificial Silk at National Exhibition: The Wuxing National Goods Mobile Exhibition in this city is located inside the National Goods Commercial Building and is participated by more than fifty vendors from other counties, along with the original stores, totaling more than eighty stalls. It opened on the 10th of this month. All goods sold by vendors were domestic products. It was discovered that the goods displayed by the four silk factories from Hangzhou participating in the exhibition, including Meifeng, Jiulun, Shuntai, and Tianjin, mainly consisted of artificial silk, which was being sold on site. The news was learned by the workers of the local silk industry. At 4 PM that afternoon, a worker representative, Xin, led more than fifty workers to the exhibition to remove and burn the artificial silk fabrics in order to promote domestic goods. At that time, the order in the exhibition hall was chaotic. Fortunately, military police were present to maintain order and prevent accidents. Construction Bureau Director Lao Naixin came forward to mediate, and the travel representative of the Hangzhou National Exhibition jointly declared on the spot that the four companies, Meifeng, Jiulun, Shuntai, and Tianjin, would be allowed to move out of the exhibition hall, and the matter was resolved. It is reported that the above four factories immediately moved their goods out and planned to return to Hangzhou.

Bandits Set Fire and Kidnap: The family of Wu Ziqi, a resident of Wujiazhu, about eight miles from Changxing, was well-off. Because bandits were rampant in the area, Wu had moved his entire family to the city last year, leaving only one worker to take care of the house. On the night of the 9th, more than twenty bandits broke into the house and searched everywhere for people and valuables. Enraged, the bandits piled the farm tools and utensils in the house in an open space and set them on fire, burning many items. They also found a worker in the woodpile, seized him, and left a threatening letter demanding a large sum of money.

Yangzhou 89

Receipt of Threatening Letter and Arrest of Suspects: The Public Security Bureau, through examination of letters, obtained a threatening letter from Sha Peizhi outside Dongguan, demanding 500 yuan, to be delivered at the Luobo Gan factory established by the Nanjing Dechang Soy Sauce Garden outside Xunningmen on the twenty-first night of the lunar month, with three flashes of a flashlight as a signal. The fourth precinct was specially ordered to investigate. Officer Huang led the police to wait on time and saw three flashes of a flashlight. They fired a gun to arrest the suspects, but the factory was tightly closed. Upon knocking, only three people were found naked in bed. After questioning their names as Zhou Santian, Da Wang, and Hongcai, it was suspected that they were the bandits. Sha was asked to identify whether there were any people with grudges among them for further verification.

Intercepted Association Money Recovered, Five Bandits Arrested: Fan Yonghai, a villager from Yangshoujian Township in Xixiang, went to Bengang on the 11th to collect association money. On his way back to the town, he was robbed of 109 yuan in his belly pocket by many bandits. He shouted for help and was beaten by the bandits. The public security station in the area sent police to protect him and arrested five suspects, Wang Changdong, Liu Changcai, Liu Zaiyu, Yin Jiujiang, and Ding Zheng'an, and turned them over to the court for interrogation.

Nantong 90

Notorious Bandit Escorted to Province for Execution: Dou Shuanglin, a notorious bandit from Tongzhou, was captured by the county government and escorted to the provincial anti-bandit headquarters for interrogation. Due to conclusive evidence, he was sentenced to death by shooting in the province and the county government was notified.

Large Group of Sea Bandits Invades Lusi Again: The sea bandits who had previously occupied Pengjiatao in Lusi Sanjia Town had been completely routed by the police and defense forces. However, the bandit leader Pan Kaiwu and others have once again led bandits to invade Lusi. Town Chief Cheng telegraphed the county government for assistance. County Magistrate Zhang sent a team to block the bandits and telegraphed the Navy Department to dispatch shallow-water warships for assistance.

Provincial Security Department Interrogates Wu and Yang: The cases of Wu Qinmian and Yang Jinyun, bandits from the Pingchao District, were released by the court without prosecution. The county government then arrested them, and the provincial security department, believing that the case involved many people, ordered the county to escort the two bandits to the department. On the 11th, police were dispatched to escort them to Zhenjiang by upstream steamer.

Tonghai Customs Cloth Business Suspended: The large-scale local cloth business in Tonghai County that transports goods to the three northeastern provinces has now reached the autumn season of closing and will be suspended immediately. It is estimated that 100,000 rolls of local cloth have been transported north this year.

Rugao 91

East Taizhou County Magistrate Discusses Coastal Defense: County Magistrate Shen of East Taizhou came to Rugao yesterday afternoon to discuss coastal defense issues in Rugao and the East China Sea. It is said that although the Pengcha pirates have been repeatedly defeated, a large number of them are still lurking in the sea.

Sea Bandits Plan to Attack Ju River Harbor: Shen Guanxi and Shen Guanshou, leaders of the Northern faction of sea bandits from Bei Pai, and Pan Wuwu, Yan Boping, and Song Lisun, leaders of the Southern faction of sea bandits, had previously engaged in infighting. It is now learned that the two factions have now negotiated a truce and plan to jointly attack Ju River Harbor.

Changsha Actively Deploys Defense: In view of the recent rampant banditry, all sectors of Changsha Town plan to cut off the traffic arteries of the village stoves, pedestrians, and crossroads. If the main points of transportation cannot be cut off, wooden sheds will be installed and soldiers will be deployed to defend them.

Ningbo 92

Yongjian Warship Returns for Repairs: The Navy Department dispatched the Lianjing and Yongjian warships to greet Chairman Jiang back to Beijing. At 9 PM on the 9th, Chairman Jiang and his wife, Kong Xiangxi and his wife, Zhu Peide, and others departed from Xikou, Fenghua, and boarded the Yongjian warship. Because Chairman Jiang and others knew that the warship's speed was slow, they switched to the Lianjing warship, and the Yongjian warship was used to escort and load luggage. It is now learned that the Yongjian warship's rudder was damaged while escorting the group to Qingshui. On the evening of that day, it turned back to 寧波 for repairs. The dozens of pieces of luggage carried by the warship were removed by the guards on the afternoon of yesterday and transferred to the Ningxing Wheel to be transferred to Beijing.

Two Young Women Kidnapped in Kaimingfang: Kaimingfang is located in the center of Ningbo and is easily accessible. Starting in February and March of last year, the old houses there were demolished and rebuilt into new-style buildings for general residency. Wang Heqing resided in No. 5 of Kaimingfang. Wang is a native of Sanbei in Zhenhai and is said to be a businessman in Shanghai. He is over fifty years old and has one son and three daughters. The eldest daughter is already married. The second daughter is twenty-nine years old and has received education. At around 3 PM on the 1st of this month, she was standing outside the door holding her three-year-old niece, looking around, when two or three kidnappers clapped her on the back. The young woman became unconscious and was taken away by the bandits. The Wang family received a letter from the bandits the next afternoon, stating: "We did not know that the child we kidnapped was a girl. Now we have kidnapped her along with the older young woman to Shanghai. We hope you will quickly prepare money to redeem them. Their lives are safe." Although the bandits sent a letter requesting money, they did not write down the redemption location. The family was very anxious after receiving the letter and telegraphed Wang Heqing in Shanghai. Wang arrived in Ningbo yesterday from Shanghai, but there is no solution at the moment. It is also said that the three-year-old girl who was kidnapped is the daughter of Wang Heqing's eldest daughter and had just come to Wang's house as a guest at the end of last month. The second daughter who was kidnapped was originally scheduled to leave in the afternoon.

Respectfully, Fengxian County Public Funds and Public Property Management Office. November 11.

Central China University Students Urge Yu Youren to Return to School 98

The League of Chinese Public School Students Yesterday Submitted a Request to the Board of Trustees, Firmly Supporting the Board's Resolutions

(National News Agency) The League of Students of the Wusong Central China University, who have resolved the student unrest, yesterday submitted a request to the school's board of trustees, expressing their firm support for the board's original resolutions and urging the new President, Yu Youren, to take office immediately. The original text reads: "Since the honorable board resolved on October 30th to approve Mr. Ma Junwu's resignation and elect Mr. Yu Youren to succeed him as President, all the students, except for a few troublemakers, have been overjoyed and celebrating. However, the next day (October 31st), a small number of troublemakers, Zhang Yaoxian, Pang Mengfei, and others, took advantage of Mr. Liu Binglin, a member of the board of trustees, coming to the school to teach economics, coercing Mr. Liu to report the truth of the board's resolution in the auditorium. They immediately seized the opportunity to announce the convening of a general assembly. Under the direction of the chief of general affairs, Wang Hongshi, with only a little over two hundred people, they dared to falsely use the name of the entire student body to forcibly pass a resolution opposing the honorable board's resolution. They also illegally produced a delegation of eleven people: Zhang Yaoxian, Li Shengjian, Pang Mengfei, Wu Moyue, Yi Yue, Ou Yingzhao, Xie Jieping, Liu Gongren, Liao Junqing, Chen Baoqiu, and Liao Lie. They established an office in the eighth classroom and organized a discipline squad to patrol day and night with wooden sticks, resulting in the genuine opinions of the majority of students being unable to be expressed. On the [blank] day of this month, the delegation again used the [blank] time to falsely report news, forcibly holding a so-called second general assembly. The number of people was only over two hundred. The delegation's [blank] discipline squad used [blank] force to guard the gate, not allowing anyone to leave their seats, and resolved to retroactively approve the transfer of student union funds, etc. On the morning of the 10th of this month, the delegation again used the [blank] time to forcibly hold a so-called third general assembly. The number of attendees was still less than three hundred, and they still forcibly held the meeting place, more clearly announcing their opposition to the honorable board's resolution, vowing to defend Mr. Ma first, and strongly resisting Mr. Yu's presidency. Furthermore, the chief of general affairs, Wang Hongshi, handed the keys to the delegation, completely sealing off the classrooms and auditorium, forcing the entire student body to strike. Such illegal behavior is truly unforgivable. After being forced to strike, the majority of students were extremely indignant and spontaneously launched a resumption of classes movement. Yesterday afternoon at four o'clock, trustees Hu Shi and Wang Yunwu came to the school to report. About five or six hundred students gathered in the auditorium to listen to the news (the auditorium can at most accommodate a little over five hundred people), which was still less than half of the entire student body. After Trustee Wang read Mr. Ma's letter, Trustee Hu immediately explained it, saying that Mr. Ma's words in the letter, 'I very much want to meet with you all,' meant that he was extremely willing to return to be President. This was already ridiculous sophistry. He also said, 'Based on my (Mr. Hu referring to himself) thirteen years of experience seeing student movements, strikes never fail. Because after a strike, the students disperse, general assemblies cannot be held, and strength cannot be expressed. Therefore, you should support Mr. Ma's reinstatement by resuming classes. I will definitely help you realize this. If the board of trustees does not allow Mr. Ma to return to school, then it will not be too late to strike, even for a year, two years, or three years,' and so on. Secretly, Mr. Hu is excessively clever. How could he possibly come up with this behavior of inciting [opposition to] the honorable board's resolution? It is truly perplexing. Finally, he claimed to have the qualifications of a former President, current trustee, and dean of the faculty of arts and sciences, and acted on behalf of the student union chairman, disregarding the students' legal questions and resolutely putting the issue of resuming classes as conditional upon Mr. Ma's reinstatement to a vote. This overstepping of boundaries is inappropriate for Mr. Hu. In short, Mr. Hu's visit to the school contains the following four suspicions: (1) Inciting students to oppose the honorable board's resolution; (2) Representing the board of trustees with the qualification of a trustee; (3) Suggesting methods for students to stir up trouble; (4) Acting on behalf of the illegal student union chairman with the qualification of a trustee, etc., monopolizing the meeting place. Mr. Hu's advice to students to resume classes is truly the wish of the entire student body, and should not be made with ulterior motives. The students vow to uphold the honorable board's original resolution and welcome Mr. Yu's presidency. We hereby respectfully submit this document to the honorable board, requesting that it firmly maintain the original resolution and urge Mr. Yu to come to school as soon as possible to formally take office. We cannot express the urgency of our request enough. Respectfully submitted to the Chairman of the Board of Trustees of the Chinese Public School, Cai [blank]."

President Li Lianggong of the Agricultural College of Labor University Sends a Letter to All Faculty and Staff 100

President Li Lianggong of the Agricultural College of Labor University respectfully addresses all faculty and staff: "Yesterday, I saw a letter from nine teachers, including Wu Shuge, Fang Cheng, and Chen Guorong, to all students of the Agricultural College. In a fit of anger, they slandered me in many ways. Currently, there are three major disputes in our school: one is the entire student body's opposition to the school affairs meeting and the expulsion of the presiding officers, Mr. Peng Xiang and Mr. Cheng Yuyun; the second is the chemistry department students' opposition to Mr. Fang Cheng and Mr. Wu Shuge; and the third is the horticulture department students' opposition to Mr. Chen Guorong. The school affairs meeting, at a critical moment, could not take the overall situation into consideration, indulging in emotional actions and rejecting Mr. Zhuang Quan as the Dean of the Engineering College, which triggered a major change and lost the students' trust. I advocate acting cautiously with the school and the studies of over a thousand young students as the premise. Instead, they accuse me of colluding with the Ministry of Education, defaming me in various ways, even abandoning lectures during class time to engage solely in personal attacks, which aroused the students' antipathy. The facts of who instigated the student unrest are clear. Mr. Fang Cheng and Mr. Wu Shuge have even come up with a novel idea, openly telling the chemistry department students that I have signed a secret treaty of twelve articles with the Ministry of Education, but have not dared to respond to the students' requests to announce the content and evidence of the so-called secret treaty, thereby exposing their lies, losing the trust of the entire department's students, and reaching the point where they cannot attend classes. In order to maintain the memorial, I still put aside personal grudges and try my best to guide the students. As for Mr. Chen Guorong being opposed by the horticulture department students, it has not been a matter of a single day, with a complex background that is painful to speak of. Mr. Chen himself is very clear about this, so Mr. Chen once proposed three conditions to me: one was to dismiss Mr. Zhang Nong, the director of the agricultural field; two was to separate the horticulture experiment from the agricultural experiment; and three was to have the horticulture department students submit letters of repentance. I replied that the first two items could be my responsibility, but there was no way to do the third item because the students had not publicly opposed him. I only made a request to the administrative side to replace the department head. Of course, the administrative side could refuse to accept it and reprimand him with righteousness, ordering him to remain as if nothing had happened, without delving deeper. Mr. Chen was not satisfied. Subsequently, Mr. Su, Zhang, Zhou, Ma and other teachers took a week off. I even ordered student representatives to request classes at Mr. Chen's and other teachers' residences. Mr. Chen remained consistently dissatisfied. Now he has joined forces with Zhang Xiannong, Sheng and others, and Wu is making things difficult for me. Isn't this ridiculous? The above is the cause and process of the disturbances. Who is attacking colleagues and who is instigating student unrest need not be inferred. As for the accusation that I am scheming for power and trying to become the President, it is extremely laughable. When Mr. Li Shizeng, Mr. Wu Zhihui, and former President Yi were in Beijing discussing with the Ministry of Education about changing the receiver to a point inspection and appointing Mr. Liu as the President, and I was temporarily acting on his behalf before Mr. Liu arrived, Mr. Peng Xiang was in Beijing and was the first to hear about it. Mr. Peng's return to school on the day I received the telegram from Mr. Li and Yi inviting me to Beijing was formally reported at the school affairs meeting. This was clearly predetermined by Mr. Li and Yi. I still felt ashamed of my lack of talent and dared not accept it, and have formally declined to Mr. Li and Yi. How could there be any scheming? And when Mr. Zhang Nong first arrived at the Agricultural College at the beginning of the summer vacation, he said to people, 'President Li's position cannot be maintained for long, and the authorities and students are looking to me.' When the news of Mr. Li and Yi's proposal to have me act as the President spread, I had not yet returned to Shanghai. Mr. Fang and Wu immediately yielded the position of Dean of the Faculty of Science. Subsequently, Mr. Fang and Zhang successively made excuses to say that they were summoned to Beijing by telegram from Mr. Yi and hid for several days. It was not until Mr. Yi returned to Shanghai that we learned that there was no telegram summoning the two gentlemen. Then, what is the meaning of scheming for power? Previously, a leaflet signed 'School Protection Group' was found on the Jiangwan campus. No one in the school had ever heard of this kind of 'School Protection Group.' The purpose of this anonymous leaflet was unfathomable at the time. Now Mr. Fang, Wu and others cite this as one of my crimes, which shows the depth of their scheming. Recently, someone even went to the Public Security Bureau to accuse me of selling soil. Police officers came to the door to search, but found nothing and left. At that time, I happened to be away from home, only frightening my old mother. I went to the bureau to inquire who had accused me. The bureau chief refused to reveal the true name, but said that he lived at a certain number in a certain neighborhood, which was already clear. Now they are citing this as one of my crimes, which further shows the insidiousness of their intentions. They are doing everything possible to fabricate and falsely accuse me, so it is no wonder that they make up groundless and baseless stories. Recently, there have been several anonymous threatening letters saying that if I do not resign from the position of President, they will use a handgun against me. These letters have all been sent to the Public Security Bureau for safekeeping. Since they have reached the point of doing anything, a violent attack is also possible. I have decided to leave Shanghai and go elsewhere. I respectfully request that all the teachers in the school jointly maintain the school affairs. The various disputes cannot be resolved until the new President arrives. I will also wait until then to submit my resignation. It is not that I dare to lightly abandon my responsibility when the turmoil has not settled, but because the cause of education is not the responsibility of one person. Since there are people among my colleagues who disregard the overall situation and only indulge in emotional actions, before the new President arrives, my staying here will not be enough to resolve the disputes. I hope that the teachers will lead the students to attend classes peacefully and wait quietly for the new President to arrive and resolve the matter. I hope you will understand my personal difficulties. I respectfully wish you all well. Your humble servant, Li Lianggong, respectfully presents this on November 13th."

Amidst the Opening of the Fourth Plenary Session, Various Sectors of This City Demand 114

The Celebration of the Premier's Birthday Committee Yesterday Sent Out Five Essential Telegrams

The representatives of various sectors of Shanghai held the 65th anniversary celebration of the Premier's birthday on the 12th of this month, and passed five major proposals, which were telegraphed by the Municipal Party Headquarters' Propaganda Department. It is understood that these telegrams were drafted by the Municipal Propaganda Department yesterday and sent separately. The original texts are recorded as follows:

Telegram Congratulating the Opening of the Fourth Plenary Session: To the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee of the Nanjing Central Committee: At this time when the great chaos has just subsided and unity has begun, your committee is convened in a timely manner to consolidate the foundation of unity and realize lasting peace. The people yearn for this, and all sides rejoice together. Recalling that since the beginning of political tutelage, due to repeated disruptions by warlords, the Central Government has been exhausted from suppressing rebellions and has not been able to focus on construction. Now that the obstacles have been removed and peace has reappeared, the members of your committee will surely be able to use their farsightedness and insight to formulate comprehensive plans for the major policies of the party and the country, to relieve the suffering of the people and complete the construction of political tutelage, to establish the foundation for national unity and peace, and to lead the nation to prosperity. We hereby send this telegram to congratulate you and express our sincerity. The Shanghai Celebration of the Premier's Birthday Conference respectfully submits.

Telegram Requesting the Elimination of Remnant Warlords: The Central Government's repeated campaigns to suppress rebellions are for the purpose of seeking genuine unity for the country and pursuing lasting peace. Without unity, political tutelage and construction cannot be carried out smoothly; without peace, the suffering of the people cannot be relieved. In recent years, if it were not for the successive rebellions of the warlords such as Yan and Feng, the construction of political tutelage would have been considerable long ago. Fortunately, Commander-in-Chief Chiang bravely suppressed the rebellion, and Vice Commander-in-Chief Zhang assisted the Central Government. The rebellions were quelled and peace was restored. As all sides celebrate the Premier's birthday, your committee is convened in the capital, and Vice Commander-in-Chief Zhang has also come south to participate in your committee, gathering comrades together to decide on the major policies of the party and the country. Hearing this good news, all are rejoicing. However, the remnant warlords in the country have not yet been eliminated, which hinders the future of political tutelage. We dare to ask your committee to order Commander-in-Chief Chiang and Vice Commander-in-Chief Zhang to use their wise and brave means to jointly eliminate the remnant warlords, and then lay the foundation for the country, bring politics back on track, and reform society, so that the whole country can enjoy the benefits of the Three Principles of the People as soon as possible. Saving the country from danger and supporting the weak, we will feel the grace of the coming rescue; restoring the country and invigorating it, we vow to exhaust our sincerity in supporting it. The Shanghai Celebration of the Premier's Birthday Conference respectfully submits.

Telegram Requesting the Elimination of Bandits and Communists in Various Places: With the defeat of Yan and Feng, the military affairs have ended, and your committee is convened in a timely manner, all are rejoicing. We believe that the implementation of all new policies depends on the stability of social order; otherwise, we will be too busy saving lives to discuss implementation. In recent years, the bandits and communists have been rampant, and there is no place that has not suffered from their harm. Society has collapsed and the people's livelihood is truly shocking. We dare to ask your committee to order the troops stationed in various places to eliminate the bandits and communists within a time limit, in order to eliminate the factors that disrupt order and destroy tranquility, and to establish a stable and strong foundation for the country and society. Then, let the people live in peace and work happily, smoothly implement new policies, vigorously promote the revitalization of agriculture, industry, and commerce, and jointly alleviate economic difficulties. Receiving these benefits, we dare not expect them without addressing them to your committee. We are overwhelmed with anticipation as we await your reply. The Shanghai Celebration of the Premier's Birthday Conference respectfully submits.

Telegram Requesting the Revision of the Sino-Dutch Treaty: To the National Government: The abolition of unequal treaties is the legacy of our Premier and has been the focus of our Central Government's efforts in foreign affairs over the years. We have learned that the Sino-Dutch consular treaty expired in August. We hope that your government will re-revise it, based on the principle of equality and mutual benefit between the two countries, and remove the shackles of the past. The Shanghai Celebration of the Premier's Birthday Conference respectfully submits.

Telegram Requesting Protest Against the Dutch Mistreatment of Overseas Chinese: To the Nanjing Ministry of Foreign Affairs: In recent years, the repeated oppression of our overseas Chinese by Dutch imperialism has been reported frequently. Recently, there have been reports of the insult of Ms. Xiao Xin'an and the expulsion of Comrade Feng Hanyue. We are all outraged. Various places have been forced by righteousness to unanimously condemn them. However, the Dutch authorities have despised our country and have not yet made any expressions. This is not only the insult of Xiao and Feng individually, but the disgrace of our entire nation. We dare to ask your ministry to promptly conduct serious negotiations with the Dutch government, seeking to punish the culprits in order to restrain the ambitions of imperialists. We are overwhelmed with anticipation as we await your reply. The Shanghai Celebration of the Premier's Birthday Conference respectfully submits.

More Chinese Laborers Deported from Japan 119

This year, due to the contraction of various factories and plants in Japan, over one thousand Chinese laborers have been laid off, unable to survive, and deported back to China. This time, seventeen Chinese laborers from Yamashita-cho and Oshima-cho in Tokyo, Japan, including Li Yanjin, Lin Qinguang, Zhuo Yunzhai, Wang Zhongdai, Xu Bingyan, Cai Sanmei, Chen Jinshi, Chen Shanfa, Wu Baofu, and Pan Ziyuan, were sent to Shanghai by the Japanese due to lack of livelihood and have already arrived in Shanghai, landing at the Wayside Wharf. The cruelty of the treatment they received from the Japanese and their miserable state upon arrival in Shanghai are difficult to describe. There are also five people, including Jiang Boqing, Xia Zhenru, and Zhang Yinkuang, who were deported to Shanghai from Nagoya. Also, a Chinese laborer who was laid off from Shimonoseki was also deported back to China.

Proposal to Change Insurance Policies to Chinese 120

Companies Must Register Before Operating

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating that insurance policies should all be in Chinese. It was reported to the relevant authorities for review and implementation. The case involves a suggestion from Supervisor Lu Qisheng of the Chamber of Commerce. In recent years, cases of insurance companies refusing to pay claims have been frequently reported, especially the case of Barreto and other insurance companies refusing to pay over 300,000 taels in Xinji insurance money to the Fuzhou community. In some cases, they used the excuse that the conditions were in foreign languages. Contracts should be made with full understanding of both parties before they are signed. However, most people in society rely on the incomplete information from insurance brokers and do not read the foreign language documents. They rashly pay the premiums and receive a piece of foreign language paper as evidence. When an incident occurs, the insurers then quote the clauses and regulations, stating how the incident is not covered or not their responsibility. This is something that the general public hates and despises. To correct the past and plan for the future, the clauses and regulations on life and fire insurance policies must be abolished and only Chinese should be used as the standard. All life and fire insurance companies, whether Chinese or foreign, must register with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government before they can operate, otherwise they should be banned. This will not only prevent civil disputes, but also recover economic losses. Therefore, it is proposed to forward this to the National Government for thorough implementation. It was discussed at the sixth executive committee meeting on the 8th of this month that the insurance business is related to the life and property of the people and is not a trivial matter. Insurance policies are a kind of contract given by the insurance company to the insured. If both parties do not understand it, it is impossible to establish trust. There are many well-established insurance companies in Shanghai, but there are also many with weak capital who use it to defraud. The insured do not know the inside story and only rely on brokers to forward the information, giving them a piece of incomprehensible foreign language document. They have no way to understand what is written in the document. The resulting abuses, such as refusing to pay claims or deducting payments, are endless and the harm is not insignificant. It was unanimously agreed that the proposal to abolish foreign languages and use Chinese for life and fire insurance policies, and that all companies, whether Chinese or foreign, should register with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce before they are allowed to operate, is indeed to correct past mistakes and safeguard national sovereignty in the future. It was unanimously decided to approve the proposal and forward it to the National Government for review and implementation. This is for the public good. Sincerely submitted to the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau.
